The service staff said that they clean the pool every night, drain it in the evening, and drain it in the morning. They took us to the hot kang to lie down for a while. When we were soaking in the hot spring, we heard the constant sound of running water. The staff said that it was hot water coming out from under the pool and the cold water was The sound of water flowing out from the overflow hole above. I saw with my own eyes the sound of water flowing out in the morning when the water was released. I felt that no matter whether the water was hot spring water or not, it was at least clean and hygienic, making people feel safe to soak in it. The service staff of the hot spring were not very good. Professional, but the service is warm and generous. There were not many people when we took a bath. The two elder sisters kept putting our slippers neatly and kept pouring water for us. From the time we entered the hot spring to the time we left, it was really It's a butler service, the restaurant is pretty good, the food is delicious, and the environment is good. Overall, I'm very satisfied and will tell people around me when I get home! Let me tell you secretly that you can park your car and drink in the hotel parking lot when you go up the mountain. Opposite the hotel is the ticket hall of the scenic spot. You can save dozens of parking fees by driving away after you go down the mountain. I suggest you stay in this hotel when you go up Huashan. It's a little more expensive, but if it's expensive, it's expensive. It's nice.
